    SELECT TOP(1) [e].[Id], [e].[City], [e].[CreatorId], [e].[Description], [e].[EndDateTime], [e].[EventCategoryId], [e].[LevelCategoryId], [e].[MaxNumberOfPlayers], [e].[Name], [e].[PriceForEvent], [e].[StartDateTime], [e].[Street], [e].[SurfaceCategoryId], [e].[SurroundingCategoryId], [u].[Id] AS [Id0], [u].[FirstName], [u].[LastName], [e0].[Id] AS [Id1], [e0].[ImageForBoxWithEventInfo], [e0].[ImageForSearchBar], [e0].[Name] AS [Name0], [l].[Id] AS [Id2], [l].[Name] AS [Name1], [s].[Id] AS [Id3], [s].[Name] AS [Name2], [s0].[Id] AS [Id4], [s0].[Name] AS [Name3]
    FROM [Events] AS [e]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [e].[CreatorId] = [u].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [EventCategories] AS [e0] ON [e].[EventCategoryId] = [e0].[Id]

) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [Registrations] AS [r] ON [t].[Id] = [r].[EventId]
